		}

		conn_class CNR.UL.N {
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.0.W.0 = IO.DOUBLE.0.N.1;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.0.W.1 = IO.DOUBLE.0.N.2;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.1.W.0 = IO.DOUBLE.1.N.1;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.1.W.1 = IO.DOUBLE.1.N.2;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.2.W.0 = IO.DOUBLE.2.N.1;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.2.W.1 = IO.DOUBLE.2.N.2;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.3.W.0 = IO.DOUBLE.3.N.1;
			reflect IO.DOUBLE.3.W.1 = IO.DOUBLE.3.N.2;
		}
	}
}
